# Plugin Directory

> The exhaustive index of every plugin in Obsidian's official `community-plugins.json` registry. Generated from upstream data, not curated.
>
> **Curated picks** with our notes and tag system live in the [main README](../README.md).
>
> Last synced: 2026-04-25 from [obsidianmd/obsidian-releases](https://github.com/obsidianmd/obsidian-releases).
> Source files: `community-plugins.json` + `community-plugin-stats.json`.

**2,750 plugins indexed.**

| [3D Graph New](https://github.com/HananoshikaYomaru/obsidian-3d-graph) | 23K | A 3D Graph view. |

| [复制图文 (Copy Image Text)](https://github.com/msgk239/obsidian-copy-image-text) | 2K | Copy note content (including text and images) to clipboard. 复制笔记内容（包括文本和图片）到剪贴板。. |
| [新枝Newledge](https://github.com/DepartingAgain/obsidian-newledge) | 1K | Import Newledge data. |
| [盘古 PanGu](https://github.com/Natumsol/obsidian-pangu) | 27K | Add spaces between Chinese characters and English alphabet. A boon for typographically compulsive people. |
